			<h1><span style=""><span style="color:black"><strong><span style="">ANH</span></strong></span></span></h1>
			</td>
			<td colspan="2" style="background-color:#ffff99; border-bottom:1px solid black; border-left:none; border-right:1px solid black; border-top:1px solid black; text-align:center; vertical-align:middle; white-space:normal; width:795px"><span style=""><span style="color:black"><strong><span style="">T&Agrave;I LIỆU ANH VĂN TỔNG HỢP</span></strong></span></span></td>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function XemTraLoi() {
        var x = document.getElementById("XemLoiGiai");
        if (x.style.display === "none") { x.style.display = "block"; } else { x.style.display = "none"; }
        var y = document.getElementById("ButtonPost");
        if (y.style.display === "none") { y.style.display = "block"; } else { y.style.display = "none"; }

        if (getCookie("Aff") == '') {
            setCookieAff("Aff", "1", 1);//https://bit.ly/3LsAgcj
            window.open('https://s.shopee.vn/6KjZ4u9Muf', '_blank');
            //setTimeout(function () { window.open('https://s.shopee.vn/6KjZ4u9Muf', '_blank'); }, 3000);

        } else {
            const d = new Date();
            var Time0 = d.getTime() / 1000;
            var Time1 = getCookie("Aff");
            var Time2 = Number(Time1);
            if (Time0 > Time2) {
                setCookieAff("Aff", "1", 1);//https://bit.ly/3LsAgcj
                window.open('https://s.shopee.vn/6KjZ4u9Muf', '_blank');
                //setTimeout(function () { window.open('https://s.shopee.vn/6KjZ4u9Muf', '_blank'); }, 3000);
            }
        }


    }

</script>
